name:Tâ€aâ€nâ€sâ€hâ€iâ€yâ€i
info:YINSHAN King
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:25 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted May 8, 2024
msg:600 acres of lake land, 144 rooms. The space is generous, with basic rooms starting from 54 square meters, and the design is simple and elegant. Youxi dining area is quiet and elegant, with a sense of Aman. The recommended guest room is the Hidden Mountain Suite, which has a 10-meter wide window and a panoramic view of the lake and mountains.
It is reported that the design inspiration comes from Xie Lingyun's "Mountain Residence", "Shangtian, Xiahu, Xixi, Nangu", etc., are all vaguely visible. The name of the store is borrowed from Xie An's famous couplet, "to entrust the true interest of the landscape and embrace the magnificent view of the sky." The word "Guan" was extended to Wang Xizhi's "Preface to the Lanting Collection", and the point on the right side of the word was taken from the first stroke of Master Hongyi's "Heart Sutra".
Such pursuit of perfection is a typical example of Chinese thinking, but in fact it goes against the elegance of the feelings of mountains and rivers. A good hotel is still a good hotel. Worth a stay.

msg:The overall environment of the hotel is okay. It is surrounded by mountains and rivers and has antique buildings. I personally think it is the standard configuration of a hotel at this price. However, the overall evaluation of the stay can only be below average. Letâ€™s talk about it in detail next.
First: During the check-in process, the details of the check-in were not provided in a sloppy manner. In order to confirm one thing, you need to ask repeatedly to find out. Compared with other hotels in the same price range, the experience is relatively inferior.
Second: Room environment. When I entered the room, I felt that the previous guest had smoked in the room. The smell of smoke had not dissipated and was rather pungent. There were unknown irritants in the room. Not long after entering the room, I started sneezing and coughing non-stop. My friend who was traveling with me was even worse. My eyes developed conjunctivitis for no apparent reason, and their eyes were painful, swollen, and had discharge.
Third: The quality of the food. Because the location of this hotel is relatively remote, food can basically only be eaten in the hotel. So the price can be imagined. I went to eat their buffet hot pot that night. I canâ€™t praise the quality of the food. The shabu-shabu meat tasted like artificial meat. The steamed shrimp noodles were not fresh. The grilled meat looked so tempting. I was really disappointed. The ingredients are not complete, even the millet is not spicy, the soy sauce is super salty, the peanut butter and sesame sauce taste like those bought in the supermarket, without any special features, and the drink supply cycle is very long. In addition, the hotel stipulates that children with a height of 120cm will be charged half price. Our little girl is 121cm tall and weighs 40 pounds. She eats very little and barely eats anything. The waiters are also unaccommodating and strictly charge 140 yuan per child. I also admire their management. Concept, impersonal. Let's talk about breakfast. There are really few types of dishes and drinks in breakfast. The taste of the dishes is also very average. The dining area and dining environment are also very simple. I personally think that the quality of this breakfast is seriously inconsistent with the price of the hotel.
Fourth: Charging piles are scarce. Friends who drive electric cars are reminded to be careful. There are really few charging piles, and the management is also very poor. Many cars are fully charged and occupy the charging position for a long time. The risk of being unable to charge is relatively high. .
